NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
DRAVIDIAN BOOK HOUSE LIMITED
Periyar Thidal, 50, E.V.K. Sampath Salai, Vepery, Chennai-600 007.
NOTICE BY COMPANY OF MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP AND APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR
At the Extraordinary General Meeting of the company duly convened and held at its roistered office on Monday the
27th February, 2012, the equity shareholders have passed special resolution for :(i) Voluntary winding up of the company under section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and for appointment
of Mr R. Paranjothy, as the Liquidator in terms of section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956 and for fixing his remuneration.
(ii) Authorizing the Liquidator to do all such acts and deeds as may be necessary fir winding up the affairs of the
company and distributing its assets.
Chennai,
8th March 2012.

for Dravidian Book House Limited,
G. SWAMIDURAI,
Director.

CHANGE OF NAME
R. Balraj was born as a male child to M. Rangaraj on 4th September 1974, residing at No. 64, Sachidhanandam Street
back side, Kosapetai, Chennai-600 012. After an elaborate Sexual Reassignment Surgery, she has been living as a female
(Reference Dr. Jayaraman, Department of Plastic Reconstructive, Faciomaxillary and Cosmetic Surgery, Kilpauk Medical
College, Chennai-600 010). The Plant surgery shows that I could be treated as a female and R. Balraj shall be known as
R. JEEVA.
Chennai,
8th March 2012.

R. BALRAJ.
